***переваливать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переваливать.html>перева́ливать</a> (28939)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевалить.html>перевали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevalítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переваливать.html>перева́ливать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereválivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевалить.html>перевали́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to shift, to roll over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переваливать.html>перева́ливать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мешок.html>мешо́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одного́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плечо.html>плеча́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́е</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereválivatʹ</b> mešók s odnovó plečá na drugóje</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to shift the sack from one shoulder to the other</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переваливать.html>перева́ливать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ответственность.html>отве́тственность</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereválivatʹ</b> otvétstvennostʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to shift the responsibility</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to cross, to get to the top</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переваривать.html>перева́ривать</a> (16082)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переваривать.html>перева́ривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevárivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переварить.html>перевари́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to overdo, to spoil by overdoing</li>
<li>to cook/boil again</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>
<ol><li>to digest</li>
<li>to stand, to bear, to stomach

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переваривать.html>перева́ривает</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on jejó ne <b>perevárivajet</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he can't stand/bear her</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ва́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ри<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вать</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:везти.html>везти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">veztí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевезти.html>перевезти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereveztí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></b>)

<li>to take across, to put across

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевезти.html>перевёз</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:река.html>ре́ку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>perevjóz</b> ix čérez réku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he put/ferried them across the river</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевернуть.html>переверну́ть</a> (3785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вернуть.html>верну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевернуть.html>переверну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevernútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перевёртывать</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переворачивать.html>перевора́чивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn around</li>
<li>to overturn, to turn over</li>
<li>to turn (a page)</li>
<li>to turn inside out</li>
<li>to turn upside down</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to turn over <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">while searching, making a mess</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to transform, to radically change</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stun</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевернуть.html>переверну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевернуться.html>переверну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevernútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перевёртываться</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">перевора́чиваться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn over, to turn round</li>
<li>to capsize, to overturn
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевернуться.html>переверну́лась</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lódka <b>perevernúlasʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the boat turned over</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевернуть.html>переверну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevernútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вера.html>ве́р</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>

Зализняка — 3b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — перевёртываться, переворачиваться.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевес.html>переве́с</a> (20946)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевес.html>переве́с</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevés</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевес.html>переве́са</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевес.html>переве́сы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевес.html>переве́сов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>preponderance, advantage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:численный.html>чи́сленный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевес.html>переве́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">číslennyj perevés</i> ― <span class="e-translation">majority, numerical superiority, superior numbers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевес.html>переве́с</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>голосо́в</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevés</b> golosóv</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">majority of votes</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороне́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевес.html>переве́с</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na jevó storoné byl <b>perevés</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the odds were in his favour</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>excess weight <i>(of luggage)</i></li></ol>

***перевесить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевесить.html>переве́сить</a> (23058)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весить.html>ве́сить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vésitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевесить.html>переве́сить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevésitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переве́шивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hang in a different place</li>
<li>to weigh again, to reweigh</li>
<li>to outweigh</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take precedence, to be more significant</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***перевестись.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевестись.html>перевести́сь</a> (15656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевести.html>перевести́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevestí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевестись.html>перевести́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevestísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переводиться.html>переводи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to transfer <i>(to another place of work, study etc)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевестись.html>перевёлся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> о́мска <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> сара́тов</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>perevjólsja</b> iz Ómska v Sarátov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he transferred from Omsk to Saratov</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come to an end, to become extinct</li>

***перевод.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевод.html>перево́д</a> (2743)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переводить.html>переводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевод.html>перево́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevód</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевод.html>перево́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевод.html>перево́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевод.html>перево́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>transfer, transference</li>
<li>translation
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевод.html>перево́д</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>языка́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:английский.html>англи́йский</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevód</b> s rússkovo jazyká na anglíjskij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">translation from Russian to English</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>remittance</li>
<li>money order</li>
<li>switching, shunting</li>
<li>conversion</li></ol>

***переводить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переводить.html>переводи́ть</a> (3810)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:водить.html>води́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переводить.html>переводи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevodítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевести.html>перевести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to lead, to convey, to transfer, to move, to shift, to transmit, to switch</li>
<li>to translate, to interpret <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">into another language</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to remit (money)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переводить.html>переводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переводиться.html>переводи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevodítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевестись.html>перевести́сь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to transfer <i>(to another place of work, study etc)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переводиться.html>перево́дится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> о́мска <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> сара́тов</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>perevóditsja</b> iz Ómska v Sarátov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is transferring from Omsk to Saratov</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come to an end, to become extinct
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́ба</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пруд.html>пруду́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переводиться.html>перево́дится</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rýba v prudú ne <b>perevóditsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is always an abundance of fish in the pond</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деньги.html>де́ньги</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переводиться.html>перево́дятся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó dénʹgi ne <b>perevódjatsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is always in funds</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переводить.html>переводи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">perevodítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ди́ть<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ся</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:перевестись.html>перевести́сь</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>пере-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-вод-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

***перевозить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a> (11579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:возить.html>вози́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vozítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perevozítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перевезти.html>перевезти́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to transport, to carry (by vehicle), to remove, to move
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пассажир.html>пассажи́ров</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevozítʹ</b> passažírov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry passengers</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:груз.html>груз</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:железный.html>желе́зной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ге</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:водный.html>во́дным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:путь.html>путём</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevozítʹ</b> gruz po želéznoj doróge (vódnym putjóm)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to carry freight by rail (by water)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корабль.html>корабле́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevozítʹ</b> na korablé</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ship</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:перевозить.html>перевози́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:телега.html>теле́ге</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perevozítʹ</b> na telége</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cart</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take across, to put across</li></ol>

<p><b>пе<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ре.html>ре</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>зи́ть</b>
